( for dir in /workspace/include /workspace/os/unix; do \
      ls $dir/*.h ; \
  done; \
  echo "/workspace/server/mpm_fdqueue.h"; \
  for dir in /root/root/apr-1.7.4/include/apr-1 /root/root/apr-util-1.6.3/include/apr-1; do \
      ls $dir/ap[ru].h $dir/ap[ru]_*.h 2>/dev/null; \
  done; \
) | sed -e s,//,/,g | sort -u > export_files
